With this midi files a synthesizer can produce an endless number of different interpretations of a song, with different instruments and numerous sound effects. Hard or soft, shrill or harmonious, classic or capricious. \r\nA midi file is a collection of sheet music for a whole orchestra with up to 16 voices (= instruments or sounds). The notes for each voice are hold in a track and you can assign an arbitrary sound to each track to give it its specific character.
